                 <div class="txtNew" data-packed="true" id="comp-iu4q0fq2" style="top:160px;bottom:;left:553px;right:;width:355px;height:auto;position:absolute;margin-left:calc((100% - 980px) * 0.5)">
                  <p class="font_8" style="text-align:right;">
                   <span class="color_11">
                    When you visit Grace Point, you'll notice a couple of things right away.  One is that this is a place where people are very welcoming and real.  We love meeting new guests, because we remember the warm welcome we received when we first came.  Everybody comes dressed in a casual style.
                    <br/>
                    <br/>
                    Another thing you'll notice is that everything that happens here relates to God and the life you live.  What we talk and sing about relates to where we live right now – biblical, practical, relevant and understandable.
                    <br/>
                    <br/>
                    The music is spiritually uplifting and led by a band with guitars, keyboards, drums and a group of talented, faithful musicians. And we like variety – so in addition to opening our Bibles, you might see a video clip or hear a personal story to help illustrate what Scripture is teaching us.
                    <br/>
                    <br/>
                    Your children and teens will enjoy amazing programs designed just for them.  Middle and high school students join the adult service, and are encouraged to join their peers in a Student Life Group. Our pre-school and elementary school programs are staffed by some of the most dedicated (and fun) parents and staff around.  All of the children experience worship singing as well as a safe and fun lesson from God's Word.
                   </span>
                   <br/>
                  </p>
